ESSAR POWER TAMIL NADU LIMITED.
(Corporate identity No. U40106TN2007PLC062252)
Registered Office, Essar House, No. 77, C.P. Ramaswamy Road, Abhiramapuram, Chennai-600 018
PUBLIC NOTICE.
Notice is hereby given that pursuant to the provisions of Section 485 and all other applicable provisions of the Companies
Act. 1956 an Extraordinary General Meeting of the members of Essar Power Tamil Nadu Limited was duly convened on
Monday, September 17. 2012 at Tower 2, 5th Floor Equinox Business Part (Peninsula Techno Park), Off. Bandra Kuria
Complex. LBS Marg. Kurla (West), Mumbai-400 070, Maharashtra wherein a special resolution was passed for Voluntary
Winding up (as members Voluntary winding up) of the Company and one Mr. N.P. Jhaveri, having his office at 15 India
House, No. 3, 4th Floor, Kemps Corner, Mumbai 400 036 has been unanimously appointed as liquidator for the Purpose
of such Voluntary winding up.
For EASSAR POWER TAMIL NADU LIMITED.
Chennai,
8th October 2012.

(Sd.)..............................
VIJAYABHASKARA KALAKOTA REDDY,
Director.

(See Rule 315)

:

transformers, converters, transmitters, producers, manufacturers, processors,
developers, stores, carriers, importers and exporters of and dealers in electricity
or by products derived from such business.

MARS CONDUCTORS (INDIA) PVT. LTD.,
Manufacturer of: Super Enamelled Copper Wire.
Regd. Offi: 102, N.S.C. Bose Road, Chennai-600 079.
NOTICE
TO ALL THE SHAREHOLDERS
NOTICE is hereby given that an EXTRAORDINARY GENERAL MEETING of the company will be held on 24th day of
August, 2012 at 10.00 A.M. at 2/1 Krishnama Road, Nungambakkam, Chennai-600 034, to transact the following business:
SPECIAL BUSINESS:
To consider and if thought fit to pass the following resolution with or without modifications as SPECIAL RESOLUTION.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the Declaration of solvency dated July 23, 2012, made by the Board of Directors of the
Company under section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, Stating that the Company would be able to pay its debts in full
within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the Company, having its Registered office at 102, NSC
Bose Road, 1st Floor, Chennai-600 079 be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
FURTHER RESOLVED THAT Mr. Chainraj Jain, residing at 2/1 Krishnama Road, Nungambakkam, Chennai-600 034, be and
is hereby appointed as Liquidator of the Company for the purpose of winding up and to be reimbursed actual expenses
incurred in this regard.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Mr. Chainra Jain, Liquidator of the Company be and is hereby authorized and empowered to
exercise all powers as provided in section 457 of the Companies, Act, 1956 and further authorized to file all the necessary
forms, papers, returns, documents etc., as may be required, with the Register of Companies,
Tamil Nadu and/or such other authorities and / or agency (ies) as may be required, publish, issue any notices, forms
advertisements, declarations etc and to do all such other acts, deeds, matters and things as may be necessary to give effect
the forgoing resolution.
For MARS CONDUCTORS (INDIA) PRIVATE LIMITED,

Chennai,
11th October 2012.

(TARUN JAIN)
Director.
